  document.querySelectorAll(\'.sidebar-button\').forEach(button => {\n                button.classList.remove(\'active\');\n            });\n            \n            // Show selected panel\n            document.getElementById(`${panelId}Panel`).style.display = \'block\';\n            \n            // Add active class to clicked button\n            event.target.classList.add(\'active\');\n        }\n\n        // Load agents\n        async function loadAgents() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${window.API_BASE}/api/agents`);\n                const data = await response.json();\n                document.getElementById(\'agentCount\').textContent = data.agents.length;\n                renderAgents(data.agents);\n            } catch (error) {\n                addLog(`Error loading agents: ${error.message}`, \'error\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Load states\n        async function loadStates() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${window.API_BASE}/api/states`);\n                const data = await response.json();\n                document.getElementById(\'stateCount\').textContent = data.states.length;\n                renderStates(data.states);\n            } catch (error) {\n                addLog(`Error loading states: ${error.message}`, \'error\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Send terminal command\n        function sendCommand() {\n            const input = document.getElementById(\'terminalInput\');\n            const command = input.value.trim();\n            \n            if (!command) return;\n            \n            addTerminalOutput(`$ ${command}`);\n            \n            if (socket) {\n                socket.emit(\'terminal_command\', { command: command });\n            }\n            \n            input.value = \'\';\n        }\n\n        // Handle key press in terminal\n        function handleKeyPress(event) {\n            if (event.key === \'Enter\') {\n                sendCommand();\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Add terminal output\n        function addTerminalOutput(text) {\n            const terminal = document.getElementById(\'terminal\');\n            const entry = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            entry.className = \'log-entry\';\n            entry.innerHTML = `\n                <div class="timestamp">${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}</div>\n                <div class="message">${text}</div>\n            `;\n            terminal.appendChild(entry);\n            terminal.scrollTop = terminal.scrollHeight;\n        }\n\n        // Add log entry\n        function addLog(message, type = \'info\') {\n            const log = document.getElementById(\'systemLog\');\n            const entry = document.createElement(\'div\');\n            entry.style.marginBottom = \'5px\';\n            entry.style.color = type === \'error\' ? \'#ff4444\' : \'#00ff41\';\n            entry.textContent = `[${new Date().toLocaleTimeString()}] ${message}`;\n            log.insertBefore(entry, log.firstChild);\n        }\n\n        // Update status\n        function updateStatus(status) {\n            const statusElement = document.getElementById(\'systemStatus\');\n            const dot = document.querySelector(\'.status-dot\');\n            \n            statusElement.textContent = status;\n            \n            if (status === \'Connected\' || status === \'Ready\') {\n                dot.style.background = \'#00ff41\';\n            } else {\n                dot.style.background = \'#ff0000\';\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Check system status\n        async function checkStatus() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${window.API_BASE}/api/status`);\n                const data = await response.json();\n                \n                document.getElementById(\'agentCount\').textContent = data.agents_count;\n                document.getElementById(\'stateCount\').textContent = data.states_count;\n                \n                if (data.status === \'running\') {\n                    updateStatus(\'Connected\');\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                updateStatus(\'Disconnected\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Initialize on page load\n        window.addEventListener(\'load\', () => {\n            initSocket();\n            checkStatus();\n            addLog(\'System loaded\', \'info\');\n        });\n\n        // Periodically check status\n        setInterval(checkStatus, 5000);\n    </script>\n</body>\n</html>\n</full-file-rewrite>\n</function_calls>'}
